        <div class="repository-meta js-details-container Details"> 
         <div class="repository-meta-content" itemprop="about">
           Google Speech To Text API 
         </div> 
        </div> 
        <div class="js-gist-file-update-container js-task-list-container file-box"> 
         <div id="file-google_speech2text-md" class="file"> 
          <div class="file-header"> 
           <div class="file-actions"> 
            <a href="/alotaiba/1730160/raw/b982c3116fa4790a2233c02fd4cb1f413a7a00ca/google_speech2text.md" class="btn btn-sm ">Raw</a> 
           </div> 
           <div class="file-info"> 
            <span class="icon"> 
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-gist" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 12 16" width="12">
              <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7.5 5L10 7.5 7.5 10l-.75-.75L8.5 7.5 6.75 5.75 7.5 5zm-3 0L2 7.5 4.5 10l.75-.75L3.5 7.5l1.75-1.75L4.5 5zM0 13V2c0-.55.45-1 1-1h10c.55 0 1 .45 1 1v11c0 .55-.45 1-1 1H1c-.55 0-1-.45-1-1zm1 0h10V2H1v11z" />
             </svg> </span> 
            <a class="tooltipped tooltipped-s css-truncate" aria-label="Permalink" href="#file-google_speech2text-md"> <strong class="user-select-contain gist-blob-name css-truncate-target"> google_speech2text.md </strong> </a> 
           </div> 
          </div> 
          <div id="readme" class="readme blob instapaper_body"> 
           <article class="markdown-body entry-content" itemprop="text">
            <h1><a href="#google-speech-to-text-api" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-google-speech-to-text-api">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
               <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
              </svg></a>Google Speech To Text API</h1> 
            <p>Base URL: <a href="https://www.google.com/speech-api/v1/recognize">https://www.google.com/speech-api/v1/recognize</a><br> It accepts <code>POST</code> requests with voice file encoded in FLAC format, and query parameters for control.</p> 
            <h2><a href="#query-parameters" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-query-parameters">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
               <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
              </svg></a>Query Parameters</h2> 
            <p><code>client</code><br> The client's name you're connecting from. For spoofing purposes, let's use <code>chromium</code></p> 
            <p><code>lang</code><br> Speech language, for example, <code>ar-QA</code> for Qatari Arabic, or <code>en-US</code> for U.S. English</p> 
            <p><code>maxresults</code><br> Maximum results to return for utterance</p> 
            <h2><a href="#post" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-post">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
               <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
              </svg></a>POST</h2> 
            <p><code>body</code><br> Should contain FLAC formatted voice binary</p> 
            <h2><a href="#http-header" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-http-header">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
               <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
              </svg></a>HTTP Header</h2> 
            <p><code>Content-Type</code><br> Should be <code>audio/x-flac; rate=16000;</code>, where MIME and sample rate of the FLAC file is included</p> 
            <p><code>User-Agent</code><br> Can be the client's user agent string, for spoofing purposes, we'll use Chrome's</p> 
            <h2><a href="#examples" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-examples">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
               <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
              </svg></a>Examples</h2> 
            <p>These examples assume you have a voice file encoded in FLAC called <code>alsalam-alikum.flac</code>.</p> 
            <h3><a href="#wget" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-wget">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
               <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
              </svg></a>wget</h3> 
            <p>This will save JSON response in a file called <code>recognized.json</code></p> 
            <pre><code>wget --post-file='alsalam-alikum.flac' \
--user-agent='Mozilla/5.0 (Macintosh; Intel Mac OS X 10_6_8) AppleWebKit/535.7 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/16.0.912.77 Safari/535.7' \
--header='Content-Type: audio/x-flac; rate=16000;' \
-O 'recognized.json' \
'https://www.google.com/speech-api/v1/recognize?client=chromium&amp;lang=ar-QA&amp;maxresults=10'
</code></pre> 
            <h3><a href="#curl" aria-hidden="true" class="anchor" id="user-content-curl">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link" height="16" version="1.1" viewbox="0 0 16 16" width="16">
               <path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path>
              </svg></a>curl</h3> 
            <pre><code>curl -X POST \
--data-binary @alsalam-alikum.flac \
--user-agent 'Mozilla/5.0 (Macintosh; Intel Mac OS X 10_6_8) AppleWebKit/535.7 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/16.0.912.77 Safari/535.7' \
--header 'Content-Type: audio/x-flac; rate=16000;' \
'https://www.google.com/speech-api/v1/recognize?client=chromium&amp;lang=ar-QA&amp;maxresults=10'
</code></pre> 
           </article> 
          </div> 
         </div> 
        </div>

                short shortVal = bb.getShort();
                sampleData[x] = shortVal;

             <h3 class="timeline-comment-header-text f5 text-normal"> <strong> <a href="/code5381" class="author">code5381</a> </strong> commented <a href="#gistcomment-1223888" class="timestamp">

            <div class="edit-comment-hide"> 
             <table class="d-block"> 
              <tbody class="d-block"> 
               <tr class="d-block"> 
                <td class="d-block comment-body markdown-body  js-comment-body"> <p>loureiromahia, You have to change the URL.</p> 
                 <ol> 
                  <li>host : <a href="https://www.google.com/speech-api/v2/recognize">https://www.google.com/speech-api/v2/recognize</a></li> 
                  <li>encoding<br> FLAC<br> Flac file; 44100Hz 32bit float, exported with Audacity. Check the audio folder in this repository for some hilarious examples.<br> Channels : 2<br> Sample Rate : 44100<br> Precision : 32-bit<br> Sample Encoding: 32-bit Float</li> 
                 </ol> <p>16-bit PCM<br> The following audio options are confirmed working for 16-bit PCM sample encoding:<br> Channels : 1<br> Sample Rate : 16000<br> Precision : 16-bit<br> Sample Encoding: 16-bit Signed Integer PCM</p> 
                 <ol> 
                  <li>key<br> AIzaSyCnl6MRydhw_5fLXIdASxkLJzcJh5iX0M4</li> 
                 </ol> <p>For example(AS3)</p> <p>.<br> .<br> .<br> var PATH:String = "<a href="https://www.google.com/speech-api/v2/recognize?output=json&amp;lang=en_US&amp;key=AIzaSyCnl6MRydhw_5fLXIdASxkLJzcJh5iX0M4">https://www.google.com/speech-api/v2/recognize?output=json&amp;lang=en_US&amp;key=AIzaSyCnl6MRydhw_5fLXIdASxkLJzcJh5iX0M4</a>";<br> var urlRequest:URLRequest = new URLRequest(PATH);<br> var urlLoader:URLLoader = new URLLoader();<br> urlRequest.contentType = "audio/x-flac; rate=44100";<br> //urlRequest.contentType = "audio/l16; rate=16000";<br> urlRequest.data = flacData;<br> urlRequest.method = URLRequestMethod.POST;<br> urlLoader.dataFormat = URLLoaderDataFormat.TEXT;<br> urlLoader.addEventListener(Event.COMPLETE, urlLoader_complete);<br> urlLoader.addEventListener(ErrorEvent.ERROR, urlLoader_error);<br> urlLoader.load(urlRequest);<br> .<br> .<br> .</p> <p><a href="http://storyjava.tistory.com/">http://storyjava.tistory.com/</a> (Korean)<br> <a href="https://github.com/gillesdemey/google-speech-v2">https://github.com/gillesdemey/google-speech-v2</a></p> <p>Good luck!</p> </td> 
               </tr> 
              </tbody> 
             </table> 
            </div>

My C# snippet is this:</p> <pre><code>            using (HttpWebResponse HWR_Response = (HttpWebResponse)_HWR_SpeechToText.GetResponse ())
                            if (HWR_Response.StatusCode == HttpStatusCode.OK) {
                                    string line;
                                    using (SR_Response = new StreamReader (HWR_Response.GetResponseStream ())) {
                                            line = SR_Response.ReadToEnd ();
                                    }

                                    SR_Response.Close ();
</code></pre> </td>

             <h3 class="timeline-comment-header-text f5 text-normal"> <strong> <a href="/Kaspler" class="author">Kaspler</a> </strong> commented <a href="#gistcomment-1233366" class="timestamp">
               <relative-time datetime="2014-05-22T09:45:09Z">
                May 22, 2014
               </relative-time></a> </h3> 
            </div> 
            <div class="edit-comment-hide"> 
             <table class="d-block"> 
              <tbody class="d-block"> 
               <tr class="d-block"> 
                <td class="d-block comment-body markdown-body  js-comment-body"> <p><a href="https://github.com/akifnaeem21" class="user-mention">@akifnaeem21</a></p> <p>I'm in same situation as you - need to finish my BS project till the end of May.<br> I also was working fine with V1 till now... Anyway, now, thanks to this page and all the comments here I managed to make it work with V2.</p> <p>Here is my C# code (it's just a prototype where I tested, so it's simple):</p> <pre><code>
using System;
using System.IO;
using System.IO.Compression;
using System.Net;


class Program
{
    static void Main(string[] args)
    {
        using (var fileStream = new FileStream(@"C:\LetsArrangeMeeting.flac", FileMode.Open))
        {
            const string requestUrl = "https://www.google.com/speech-api/v2/recognize?output=json&amp;lang=en-us&amp;key=KEY_GOES_HERE&amp;client=chromium&amp;maxresults=6&amp;pfilter=2";
            var request = (HttpWebRequest)WebRequest.Create(requestUrl);
            ConfigureRequest(request);
            var requestStream = request.GetRequestStream();

            CopyStream(fileStream, requestStream);

            using (var response = request.GetResponse())
            {
                using (var responseStream = response.GetResponseStream())
                {
                    using (var zippedStream = new GZipStream(responseStream, CompressionMode.Decompress))
                    {
                        using (var sr = new StreamReader(zippedStream))
                        {
                            var res = sr.ReadToEnd();
                            Console.WriteLine(res);
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        Console.ReadLine();
    }

    private static void CopyStream(FileStream fileStream, Stream requestStream)
    {
        var buffer = new byte[32768];
        int read;
        while ((read = fileStream.Read(buffer, 0, buffer.Length)) &gt; 0)
        {
            requestStream.Write(buffer, 0, read);
        }
    }

    private static void ConfigureRequest(HttpWebRequest request)
    {
        request.KeepAlive = true;
        request.SendChunked = true;
        request.ContentType = "audio/x-flac; rate=44100";
        request.UserAgent =
            "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.2; WOW64) AppleWebKit/535.2 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/15.0.874.121 Safari/535.2";
        request.Headers.Set(HttpRequestHeader.AcceptEncoding, "gzip,deflate,sdch");
        request.Headers.Set(HttpRequestHeader.AcceptLanguage, "en-GB,en-US;q=0.8,en;q=0.6");
        request.Headers.Set(HttpRequestHeader.AcceptCharset, "ISO-8859-1,utf-8;q=0.7,*;q=0.3");
        request.Method = "POST";
    }
}

</code></pre> <p>And this is the result:</p> <pre><code>
{"result":[]}
{"result":[{"alternative":[{"transcript":"hello let's arrange a meeting in Tel Aviv at 5 o'clock"},{"transcript":"hello lets arrange a meeting in Tel Aviv at 5 o'clock"},{"transcript":"hello let's arrange a meeting in Tel Aviv at 5 o'clock Buy"},{"transcript":"hello lips arrange a meeting in Tel Aviv at 5 o'clock"},{"transcript":"hello let's arrange a meeting in Tel Aviv at 5 o'clock by"},{"transcript":"hello let's arrange a meeting in Tel Aviv at 5 o'clock buy"}],"final":true}],"result_index":0}

</code></pre> <p>Hope this helps!</p> </td> 
               </tr> 
              </tbody> 
             </table> 
            </div>

            <div class="edit-comment-hide"> 
             <table class="d-block"> 
              <tbody class="d-block"> 
               <tr class="d-block"> 
                <td class="d-block comment-body markdown-body  js-comment-body"> <p>Working java code:</p> <p>//libs to import<br> import java.io.BufferedReader;<br> import java.io.DataOutputStream;<br> import java.io.InputStreamReader;<br> import java.net.URL;<br> import java.nio.file.Files;<br> import java.nio.file.Paths;</p> <pre><code>/**
 * Send post to google
 */
private void sendPost() throws Exception {
    String USER_AGENT = "Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 6.2; WOW64) AppleWebKit/535.2 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/15.0.874.121 Safari/535.2",
    url = "https://www.google.com/speech-api/v2/recognize?output=json&amp;lang=ru-RU&amp;key=AIzaSyBOti4mM-6x9WDnZIjIeyEU21OpBXqWBgw&amp;client=chromium&amp;maxresults=6&amp;pfilter=2";

    URL obj = new URL(url);
    HttpsURLConnection con = (HttpsURLConnection) obj.openConnection();

    // add reuqest header
    con.setRequestMethod("POST");
    con.setRequestProperty("User-Agent", USER_AGENT);
    con.setRequestProperty("Content-Type", "audio/l16; rate=16000");
    con.setRequestProperty("AcceptEncoding", "gzip,deflate,sdch");

    // Send post request
    con.setDoOutput(true);
    DataOutputStream wr = new DataOutputStream(con.getOutputStream());
    wr.write(Files.readAllBytes(Paths
            .get("C:\\tmp\\test_sounds\\1_16000.wav")));
    wr.flush();
    wr.close();

    int responseCode = con.getResponseCode();
    System.out.println("\nSending 'POST' request to URL : " + url);
    System.out.println("Response Code : " + responseCode);

    BufferedReader in = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(
            con.getInputStream()));
    String inputLine;
    StringBuffer response = new StringBuffer();

    while ((inputLine = in.readLine()) != null) {
        response.append(inputLine);
    }
    in.close();

    // print result
    System.out.println(response.toString());

}
</code></pre> </td> 
               </tr> 
              </tbody> 
             </table> 
            </div> 
           </div> 
          </div>

                 <div class="highlight highlight-source-ruby">
                  <pre>        url <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>https://www.google.com/speech-api/v2/recognize?output=json&amp;lang=en-us&amp;key=AIzaSyBOti4mM-6x9WDnZIjIeyEU21OpBXqWBgw&amp;results=6&amp;pfilter=2<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
        uri <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">URI</span>.parse(url)
        http <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">Net</span>::<span class="pl-c1">HTTP</span>.<span class="pl-k">new</span>(uri.host, uri.port)
        http.use_ssl <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span>
        http.verify_mode <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">OpenSSL</span>::<span class="pl-c1">SSL</span>::<span class="pl-c1">VERIFY_NONE</span>    
        request <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">Net</span>::<span class="pl-c1">HTTP</span>::<span class="pl-c1">Post</span>.<span class="pl-k">new</span>(uri.request_uri)
        request.body <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-c1">File</span>.read(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>your_flac_file.flac}<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)
        request.content_type <span class="pl-k">=</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>audio/x-flac; rate=16000;<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>
        res <span class="pl-k">=</span> http.request(request)</pre>

                <td class="d-block comment-body markdown-body  js-comment-body"> <p>Hello everybody,</p> <p>Some time ago I created this shell script which packages everything you need to use the API v2 (record data for a given duration or use a file, specify language, filter out results, etc.): <a href="https://github.com/amsehili/gspeech-rec">https://github.com/amsehili/gspeech-rec</a></p> <p>For more details about the reverse engineering being used, check out this article: <a href="https://aminesehili.wordpress.com/2015/02/08/on-the-use-of-googles-speech-recognition-api-version-2/">https://aminesehili.wordpress.com/2015/02/08/on-the-use-of-googles-speech-recognition-api-version-2/</a></p> <p>Cheers!</p> </td> 
               </tr> 
              </tbody> 
             </table>

             <table class="d-block"> 
              <tbody class="d-block"> 
               <tr class="d-block"> 
                <td class="d-block comment-body markdown-body  js-comment-body"> <pre><code>    public static async Task&lt;string&gt; RequestGoogleSpeechAPIAsync(byte[] byteArray) 
    {
        var httpClient = new HttpClient();
        var mediaType = new MediaTypeWithQualityHeaderValue("audio/x-flac");
        var parameter = new NameValueHeaderValue("rate", "16000");
        mediaType.Parameters.Add(parameter);

        var url = "https://www.google.com/speech-api/v2/recognize?output=json&amp;lang=en-US&amp;key=";
        var appSettings = ConfigurationManager.AppSettings;
        var apiKey = "AIzaSyBOti4mM-6x9WDnZIjIeyEU21OpBXqWBgw";
        var uri = new Uri(url + apiKey);

        using (MemoryStream ms = new MemoryStream(byteArray, 0, byteArray.Length))
        {
            var param = new StreamContent(ms);
            param.Headers.ContentType = mediaType;

            var result = await httpClient.PostAsync(uri, param);

            var responseFromServer = await result.Content.ReadAsStringAsync();
            var responseArray = responseFromServer.Split('\n');
            var responseJson = await Task.Factory.StartNew(() =&gt; JsonConvert.DeserializeObject&lt;SpajamHonsen.Models.GoogleSpeechAPIResponseModel.Resuls&gt;(responceArray[1]));

            return responseJson.result[0].alternative[0].transcript;
        }
    }
</code></pre> </td>
